class=\'post-author\'><a href=\'https://www.blogger.com/profile/10752392803353895959\' target=\'_blank\' title=\'Champak&#39;s World\'>Champak\'s World</a></span>\n<span class=\'post-date published\' The application will consist of a series of multiple choice questions.
